    function isIE() {

    function sendAbTestingPageViewEvent() {
        if (window.hasOwnProperty('_gcol')) {
            const now = new Date().getTime().toString();
    
            const Ab = getCookieValue("AbTesting") || '';
            const msearchAb = getCookieValue("msearchAb") || '';
            const recoAb = getCookieValue("recoAb") || '';
            const janusAbTestCookieValue = Ab.split("|")[0];

            const abTestingCookieValue = [msearchAb, recoAb, janusAbTestCookieValue].filter(Boolean).join('-');
    
            if (!abTestingCookieValue) {
                return;
            }

            const eventData = {
                ts: now,
                channel: 'web',
                event: 'ty_analytics',
                tv007: '0',
                tv019: window.location.href,
                tv020: window.TYPageName || window.page_type || window.pageType,
                tv037: now,
                tv066: window.navigator.userAgent,
                tv230: 'WEBABTEST',
                tv231: 'ty_assignmentapi',
                tv232: janusAbTestCookieValue
            };
            
            window._gcol.Fire("ty_analytics", eventData);
        }
    }

  function getCookie(name) {
    const match = document.cookie.match(
      new RegExp("(^| )" + name + "=([^;]+)")
    );
    return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[2]) : null;
  }

  function setCookie(name, value, days) {
    let expires = "";
    if (days) {
      let date = new Date();
      date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

      expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie =
      name +
      "=" +
      encodeURIComponent(value) +
      expires +
      "; path=/; SameSite=Lax; domain=.trendyol.com";
  }

    <script>
        function registerWorker() {
            var userLoggedIn = window.userObject && window.userObject.user_customerid;
            
            if (window.SharedWorker && userLoggedIn) {
                 var url = new URL(location.href).origin + '/bundles/sync-user-worker.min.js';
                 var worker = new SharedWorker(url);
                 worker.port.postMessage({type: 'init' , interval: 0.5 });   
            }
        }
        
        window.addEventListener('load', function () {
          registerWorker()
        });
    </script>

  const demeterScript = document.createElement('script');
  demeterScript.defer = true;
  demeterScript.src = "https://cdn.dsmcdn.com/sfint/production/demeter-prod-1-1-0.umd.js";
  const janusAbTestingValue = janusAbTestingCookies || getJanusAbTestingCookies() || "empty";
  const config = {
    baseUrl: "https://demeter-tr-core-collect.trendyol.com",

  };

  demeterScript.onload = async () => {
    const demeterInstance = new window.Demeter({ config });
    try {
      await demeterInstance.init();
      window.dispatchEvent(new Event("demeterReady"));
    } catch (e) {
      console.log(e);
    }
  };
  document.body.appendChild(demeterScript);
